Key_NNP differences_NNS between_IN UK_NNP GAAP_NNP and_CC IFRS_NNP Based_VBD on_IN the_DT Groups_NNS initial_JJ assessment_NN ,_, we_PRP believe_VBP that_IN the_DT major_JJ impacts_NNS on_IN net_JJ profit_NN and_CC shareholders_NNS funds_NNS will_MD be_VB in_IN the_DT following_VBG areas_NNS ._.

Financial_NNP instruments_NNS Derivative_JJ financial_JJ instruments_NNS are_VBP used_VBN to_TO manage_VB exposure_NN to_TO foreign_JJ exchange_NN and_CC interest_NN rate_NN risks_NNS ._.

Hedge_VB accounting_NN permissibility_NN is_VBZ much_RB more_RBR restricted_VBN under_IN IAS_NNP 39_CD than_IN at_IN present_JJ under_IN UK_NNP GAAP_NNP specific_JJ designation_NN and_CC effectiveness_NN criteria_NNS must_MD be_VB satisfied_VBN ._.

The_DT Group_NNP has_VBZ and_CC continues_VBZ to_TO hedge_VB underlying_VBG exposures_NNS in_IN an_DT efficient_JJ ,_, commercial_JJ and_CC structured_JJ manner_NN ._.

60_CD Adoption_NN of_IN International_NNP Financial_NNP Reporting_NNP Standards_NNP Post_NNP employment_NN benefits_NNS Under_IN UK_NNP GAAP_NNP ,_, the_DT Group_NNP accounts_NNS for_IN its_PRP$ pension_NN costs_NNS under_IN SSAP_NNP 24_CD Accounting_NNP for_IN Pension_NNP Costs_NNS ._.

All_DT of_IN the_DT items_NNS recognized_VBN in_IN the_DT profit_NN and_CC loss_NN account_NN under_IN FRS_NNP 17_CD are_VBP treated_VBN in_IN a_DT similar_JJ way_NN under_IN IAS_NNP 19_CD ._.
However_RB ,_, actuarial_JJ gains_NNS and_CC losses_NNS that_WDT are_VBP recognized_VBN immediately_RB in_IN the_DT statement_NN of_IN total_JJ recognized_VBN gains_NNS and_CC losses_NNS under_IN FRS_NNP 17_CD are_VBP instead_RB recognized_VBN in_IN the_DT profit_NN and_CC loss_NN account_NN under_IN IAS_NNP 19_CD ,_, usually_RB over_IN a_DT period_NN representing_VBG the_DT expected_VBN average_JJ remaining_VBG working_VBG lives_NNS of_IN employees_NNS participating_VBG in_IN the_DT scheme_NN ._.

The_DT recognized_VBN asset_NN or_CC liability_NN will_MD be_VB subject_JJ to_TO changes_NNS in_IN value_NN that_WDT may_MD be_VB more_RBR volatile_JJ than_IN that_DT currently_RB recognized_VBN under_IN SSAP_NNP 24_CD ._.
This_DT volatility_NN can_MD be_VB recognized_VBN through_IN direct_JJ recognition_NN in_IN the_DT profit_NN and_CC loss_NN account_NN or_CC through_IN the_DT corridor_NN approach_NN described_VBD above_IN ._.

Intangible_JJ fixed_JJ assets_NNS -_: goodwill_NN Under_IN UK_NNP GAAP_NNP ,_, the_DT Group_NNP amortises_VBZ goodwill_NN on_IN a_DT straight_JJ line_NN basis_NN over_IN its_PRP$ useful_JJ economic_JJ life_NN ,_, a_DT period_NN not_RB exceeding_VBG 20_CD years_NNS ._.
Under_IN IFRS_NNP 3_NNP Business_NNP Combinations_NNPS ,_, goodwill_NN will_MD no_RB longer_RB be_VB amortised_VBN ,_, but_CC instead_RB will_MD be_VB subject_JJ to_TO an_DT annual_JJ impairment_NN test_NN ._.

This_DT will_MD remove_VB the_DT amortisation_NN charge_NN from_IN the_DT profit_NN and_CC loss_NN account_NN ,_, although_IN if_IN any_DT impairment_NN losses_NNS are_VBP indicated_VBN ,_, they_PRP would_MD be_VB recorded_VBN in_IN the_DT profit_NN and_CC loss_NN account_NN ._.
Intangible_JJ fixed_JJ assets_NNS -_: other_JJ IAS_NNP 38_CD Intangible_JJ assets_NNS provides_VBZ more_RBR detailed_JJ guidance_NN on_IN intangible_JJ assets_NNS than_IN UK_NNP GAAP_NNP requiring_VBG the_DT Group_NNP to_TO recognize_VB ,_, capitalize_VB and_CC amortise_VB other_JJ intangibles_NNS on_IN the_DT balance_NN sheet_NN providing_VBG they_PRP meet_VBP certain_JJ criteria_NNS ._.

Under_IN IAS_NNP 10_CD Events_NNS after_IN the_DT Balance_NNP Sheet_NNP Date_NNP ,_, the_DT dividend_NN cost_NN will_MD be_VB accounted_VBN for_IN in_IN the_DT period_NN in_IN which_WDT they_PRP are_VBP declared_VBN and_CC approved_VBN ._.
Share_NN based_VBN payments_NNS Under_IN current_JJ UK_NNP GAAP_NNP ,_, the_DT Group_NNP recognizes_VBZ a_DT charge_NN in_IN the_DT profit_NN and_CC loss_NN account_NN for_IN its_PRP$ share_NN option_NN schemes_NNS based_VBN on_IN the_DT difference_NN between_IN the_DT exercise_NN price_NN of_IN the_DT award_NN and_CC the_DT share_NN price_NN at_IN the_DT date_NN of_IN grant_NN the_DT intrinsic_JJ value_NN ._.
